<div class="tab-pane  fade tabContentPane accordionOne pageTabContentWithSideBar " id="courseInfoTab" test-id="courseInfoTab">
	
			
				
			
			<div class="wikiContent hidden"><p></p>
<div title="Course Objective~" class="chapter">
 <h2 id="section---CourseObjective">Course Objective</h2> 
 <p>The course objective of Business 101: Principles of Management (SDCM-0006) is to gain an understanding of business management, including historical and current management theory, types of managers and roles of managers in an organization. </p> 
 <p></p>
</div>
<p></p>
<p></p>
<div title="Scoring Policy~" class="chapter">         
 <h2 id="section---GradingPolicy">Grading Policy</h2>
 <table class="wikitable" border="1">
  <tbody>
   <tr>
    <th class="odd">Assignment</th>
    <th class="odd">Points</th>
   </tr>
   <tr>
    <td class="odd">Chapter Tests</td>
    <td class="odd">200</td>
   </tr>
   <tr>
    <td class="odd">Final Exam</td>
    <td class="odd">100</td>
   </tr>
  </tbody>
 </table>
</div>
<p></p>
<p></p>
<div title="Outcomes &amp; Format~" class="chapter">
 <h2 id="section---CourseOutcomes">Course Outcomes</h2> 
 <p>Upon completion of this course, you will be able to: </p> 
 <ul>
  <li>Identify the levels, roles, and functions of management. </li>
  <li>Describe past and modern theories of management, including quality management and systems management theory. </li>
  <li>Explain leading as a management function and how it affects the business organization. </li>
  <li>Analyze different types of organizational structures, including centralized and decentralized organizations, and the communication processes within these structures. </li>
  <li>Explain the differences and similarities of leaders and managers and how their roles impact an organization. </li>
  <li>Describe the role of motivation in the workplace and how managers affect motivation. </li>
  <li>Explain the process of controlling in management and decision-making, including the tools used to make informed decisions. </li>
  <li>Summarize the importance of business ethics in contemporary business. </li>
 </ul>
 <h3 id="section---Prerequisites">Prerequisites</h3> 
 <p>There are no prerequisites for this course. </p> 
 <h2 id="section---CourseFormat">Course Format</h2> 
 <p>Business 101 consists of short video lessons that are organized into topical chapters. Each video is approximately 5-10 minutes in length and comes with a quick quiz to help you measure your learning. The course is completely self-paced. Watch lessons on your schedule whenever and wherever you want. </p> 
 <p>At the end of each chapter, you can complete a chapter test to see if you're ready to move on or have some material to review. Once you've completed the entire course, take the practice test and use the study tools in the course to prepare for the final exam. You may take the final exam whenever you are ready. </p> 
 <p></p>
</div>
<p></p>
<p></p>
<div title="How It Works~" class="chapter">
 <h2 id="section---HowCreditRecommendationsWork">How Credit Recommendations Work</h2> 
 <p>This course has been evaluated and recommended by both ACE and NCCRS for 3 semester hours in the lower division baccalaureate degree category. To apply for transfer credit, follow these steps: </p> 
 <ul>
  <li>If you already have a school in mind, check with the registrar to see if the school will grant credit for courses recommended by either ACE or NCCRS. </li>
  <li>Complete Business 101 by watching video lessons and taking short quizzes. </li>
  <li>Take the Business 101 final exam directly on the Study.com site. </li>
  <li>Request a transcript to be sent to the accredited school of your choice! </li>
  <li>Check out <a class="external" href="https://study.com/academy/college-accelerator-hub/how-to-transfer-college-credit-earned-on-studycom.html">this page</a> for more information on Study.com's credit-recommended courses. </li>
 </ul>
 <h2 id="section---AdditionalInformation">Additional Information</h2> 
 <ul>
  <li><a class="external" href="https://study.com/academy/popular/studycoms-academic-integrity-policy.html">Academic Integrity Policy</a> </li>
  <li><a class="external" href="https://study.com/academy/popular/accessibility-and-disability-accommodations-at-studycom.html">Accessibility and Disability Accommodations</a> </li>
  <li><a class="external" href="https://study.com/pages/privacy_policy.html">Study.com Privacy Policy</a> </li>
  <li><a class="external" href="http://support.study.com/support/solutions/articles/1000037984-what-technology-does-study-com-support-">Required Technology for Using Study.com</a> </li>
  <li><a class="external" href="https://study.com/contact/index.html">Tech Support</a> </li>
 </ul>

<div title="Course Topics~" class="chapter">
 <h2 id="section---CourseTopics">Course Topics</h2> 
 <p></p> 
 <table class="wikitable" border="1">
  <tbody>
   <tr class="odd">
    <th>Category </th>
    <th>Objectives</th>
   </tr> 
   <tr>
    <td> Management Basics </td>
    <td> Look at the levels of management. Examine Henry Mintzberg's roles of management and explore the four functions of management.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr class="odd">
    <td> Classical School of Management Theory </td>
    <td> Dig into the classical management theory and how it developed. Study the work of Max Weber, Fredrick Taylor, Henry Gantt, and Frank and Lillian Gilbreth.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr>
    <td> Planning </td>
    <td> Compare and contrast several of the major approaches to managerial planning, understand the benefits and detriments of each, and understand which approach might be most useful in a given situation.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr class="odd">
    <td> Organizational Change </td>
    <td> Define types of internal organization change and steps in the planned change process. Discuss and compare various types of change models.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr>
    <td> Organizing in Business Management </td>
    <td> Understand the differences between organic and mechanistic organizational business structures. Identify work specializations and examine authority in organizations through concepts including delegation and span of control.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr class="odd">
    <td> Work Teams </td>
    <td> Learn about types of work teams and stages of group development. Explore group think and causes of conflict within a team.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr>
    <td> Leading in Organizations </td>
    <td> Get information on the role of leaders in an organization, with lessons on various types of leadership styles and types of power.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr class="odd">
    <td> Leadership Theory </td>
    <td> Find out about theories and models of leadership styles and when they can be effective.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr>
    <td> Motivation in the Workplace </td>
    <td> Learn about needs-based and behavior-based theories of motivation. Go over several theories of employee motivation and ways to empower employees to increase performance.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr class="odd">
    <td> Communication in the Workplace </td>
    <td> Discuss the importance of good workplace communication, and look at various types of communication used by managers. Learn about conflict management, including mediation and arbitration.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr>
    <td> Controlling in Organizations </td>
    <td> Find out about financial and budget controls in organizations.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr class="odd">
    <td> Human Resources </td>
    <td> Delve into the role of the human resources manager in an organization, with a look at hiring, new employee orientation, training programs, performance appraisals, compensation and employee termination. Learn about legal issues in human resources.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr>
    <td> Strategic Management and Managerial Decision Making </td>
    <td> Explore the four steps of the strategic management planning process and the four functions of management. Get information on what impacts decision making and learn what a PERT analysis is and how to use it.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr class="odd">
    <td> Production and Quality Assurance </td>
    <td> Learn how managers influence productivity, quality and profitability. See what the five principles of Total Quality Management are and how to use them.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr>
    <td> International Management and Contemporary Issues </td>
    <td> Find out about how the role of management differs when working in global commerce, with a careful look at ethics, economics, politics and social responsibility.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr class="odd">
    <td> Behavioral School of Management Theory </td>
    <td> Learn about several behavior theories of management, including the neoclassical theory, behavioral management theory and the needs theory. Examine the Hawthorne studies on productivity, and look at Douglas McGregor's ideas on self-fulfilling management prophecies.</td>
   </tr> 
   <tr>
    <td> Contemporary and Future School of Management Theory </td>
    <td> Explore current thought regarding managements, such as the quantitative approach and the contingency approach. Get information on systems management theory.</td>
   </tr> 
  </tbody>
 </table>
 <p></p>
</div>
<p></p></div>

	<script type="text/javascript">
		(function() {
			var crazyEggAlreadyLoaded = !!window.CE2;
			var existingCrazyEggReadyFunc = window.CE_READY;
			
			var tags = "visited_course, visited_studying_course".split(",").map(s => (s ?? "").trim());
			
			function addTagsToCrazyEgg() {
				CE2.addTag(tags);
				CE2.set(1, tags.join(", ")); // add custom user variable as well as tags - CE doesn't always support tags in the places we want them
			}
			
			if (crazyEggAlreadyLoaded) {
				addTagsToCrazyEgg();
			}
			else if (existingCrazyEggReadyFunc) {
				window.CE_READY = function() {
					existingCrazyEggReadyFunc();
					addTagsToCrazyEgg();
				}
			}
			else {
				window.CE_READY = addTagsToCrazyEgg;
			}
		})();
	</script>
